CREATE TABLE [dbo].[tblUserInformation](
	[VzID] [varchar](7) NOT NULL,
	[ScreenName] [varchar](16) NOT NULL,

	[Name] [varchar](50) NULL,

(
	[VzID] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY],
UNIQUE NONCLUSTERED 
(
	[ScreenName] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]
GO

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[tblMatchInformation](
	[MatchNo] [int] NOT NULL,
	[TeamA] [varchar](15) NULL,
	[TeamB] [varchar](15) NULL,
	[MatchTime] [datetime] NULL,
	[Toss] [varchar](15) NULL,
	[Match] [varchar](15) NULL,
	[MoM] [varchar](50) NULL,
	[VENUE] [varchar](100) NULL,
	[Result] [varchar](100) NULL,
PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[MatchNo] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]
GO
SET ANSI_PADDING OFF
GO

	[Toss] [varchar](15) NULL,

	[VzId] ASC,
	[MatchNo] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]

CREATE PROC [dbo].[spUpdateTeamPoints]  
(@Team varchar(20),@Played int, @Won int, @Lost int, @Tie int, @NR int, @Pts int, @NRR decimal(5,2))
AS  
BEGIN  
  SET NOCOUNT ON  
  UPDATE dbo.tblTeamPoints  
  SET Played = @Played, Won = @Won, Lost = @Lost, Tie = @Tie, NR = @NR, Pts = @Pts, NRR = @NRR
  WHERE Team = @Team
END

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spUpdateUserMatchInfo]
(@VzId varchar(7),@MatchNo int ,@Toss varchar(15), @Match varchar(15), @MoM varchar(50), @Score int)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
   UPDATE dbo.tblUserMatchInput
    SET MatchNo = @MatchNo, Toss = @Toss, Match = @Match, Mom = @MoM, Score = @Score,
    time_stamp = getdate()
    WHERE VzId = @VzId and MatchNo = @MatchNo
END
